  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'FoodDelivery' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'FoodDelivery' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse restaurants, view menus, place food orders, track deliveries, and write reviews. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'FoodDelivery' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'FoodDelivery' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Food Delivery Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured restaurants, popular cuisines, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-restaurants** - Type: Div - Display of featured restaurant recommendations.   - **ID: browse-restaurants-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to restaurant listing page.   - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.   - **ID: active-orders-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to active orders page.  ### 2. Restaurant Listing Page - **Page Title**: Browse Restaurants - **Overview**: A page displaying all available restaurants with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: restaurants-page** - Type: Div - Container for the restaurants page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search restaurants by name or cuisine type.   - **ID: cuisine-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by cuisine (Chinese, Italian, Indian, American, etc.).   - **ID: restaurants-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying restaurant cards with logo, name, rating, and delivery time.   - **ID: view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view restaurant menu (each restaurant card has this).  ### 3. Restaurant Menu Page - **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed menu items for a specific restaurant with descriptions and prices. - **Elements**:   - **ID: menu-page** - Type: Div - Container for the menu page.   - **ID: restaurant-name** - Type: H1 - Display restaurant name.   - **ID: restaurant-info** - Type: Div - Display restaurant info (address, phone, rating).   - **ID: menu-items-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying menu items with photos, names, descriptions, and prices.   - **ID: add-to-cart-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add menu item to cart (each item has this).   - **ID: view-item-details-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view item details (each menu item has this).  ### 4. Item Details Page - **Page Title**: Item Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific menu item including ingredients and nutritional info. - **Elements**:   - **ID: item-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the item details page.   - **ID: item-name** - Type: H1 - Display item name.   - **ID: item-description** - Type: Div - Display item description and ingredients.   - **ID: item-price** - Type: Div - Display item price.   - **ID: quantity-input** - Type: Input (number) - Field to select quantity before adding to cart.   - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add item with selected quantity to cart.  ### 5. Shopping Cart Page - **Page Title**: Shopping Cart - **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option. - **Elements**:   - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.   - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with name, quantity, price, and subtotal.   - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).   - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).   - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.   - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.  ### 6. Checkout Page - **Page Title**: Checkout - **Overview**: A page for users to enter delivery information and complete order placement. - **Elements**:   - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.   - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.   - **ID: delivery-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input delivery address.   - **ID: phone-number** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.   - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, Cash, PayPal).   - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.  ### 7. Active Orders Page - **Page Title**: Active Orders - **Overview**: A page displaying current orders being prepared or delivered with tracking information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: active-orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the active orders page.   - **ID: orders-list** - Type: Div - List displaying active orders with order ID, restaurant, status, and ETA.   - **ID: track-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view detailed tracking (each order has this).   - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Preparing, On the Way, Delivered).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Order Tracking Page - **Page Title**: Track Order - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed order tracking information with delivery person details and real-time status updates. - **Elements**:   - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.   - **ID: order-details** - Type: Div - Display complete order details and timeline.   - **ID: delivery-driver-info** - Type: Div - Display delivery driver name, phone, and vehicle info.   - **ID: estimated-time** - Type: Div - Display estimated delivery time.   - **ID: order-items-list** - Type: Div - List of items in the order.   - **ID: back-to-orders** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to active orders.  ### 9. Reviews Page - **Page Title**: Order Reviews - **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews for restaurants and allowing users to write new reviews. - **Elements**:   - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.   - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with restaurant name, rating, and review text.   - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.   - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'FoodDelivery' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Restaurants Data - **File Name**: `restaurants.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00   2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00   3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00   ```  ### 2. Menus Data - **File Name**: `menus.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1   2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1   3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1   ```  ### 3. Cart Data - **File Name**: `cart.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2|2025-01-15   2|3|2|1|2025-01-16   ```  ### 4. Orders Data - **File Name**: `orders.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234   2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678   ```  ### 5. Order Items Data - **File Name**: `order_items.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2|12.99   2|1|2|1|8.99   3|2|3|1|14.99   ```  ### 6. Deliveries Data - **File Name**: `deliveries.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45   2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30   ```  ### 7. Reviews Data - **File Name**: `reviews.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12   2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13   3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15   ```

render_template(\'track_order.html\', order_details=order_details, delivery_driver=delivery_driver or {}, estimated_time=estimated_time, order_items_list=order_items_list)\n\n\n# 11. reviews_page (GET)\n@app.route(\'/reviews\')\ndef reviews_page():\n    reviews = load_reviews()\n    rating_filter_options = [\'1\', \'2\', \'3\', \'4\', \'5\']\n    selected_rating = request.args.get(\'rating\', \'\')\n\n    if selected_rating:\n        filtered_reviews = [r for r in reviews if str(r[\'rating\']) == selected_rating]\n    else:\n        filtered_reviews = reviews\n\n    return render_template(\'reviews.html\', reviews=filtered_reviews, rating_filter_options=rating_filter_options, selected_rating=selected_rating)\n\n\n# 12. write_review_page (GET, POST)\n@app.route(\'/reviews/write\', methods=[\'GET\', \'POST\'])\ndef write_review_page():\n    restaurants = load_restaurants()\n    if request.method == \'GET\':\n        restaurant_options = [{\'restaurant_id\': r[\'restaurant_id\'], \'name\': r[\'name\']} for r in restaurants]\n        return render_template(\'write_review.html\', restaurant_options=restaurant_options)\n\n    # POST: handle review submission\n    try:\n        restaurant_id = int(request.form.get(\'restaurant_id\', \'0\'))\n    except ValueError:\n        restaurant_id = 0\n    customer_name = request.form.get(\'customer_name\', \'\').strip()\n    rating = request.form.get(\'rating\', \'\').strip()\n    review_text = request.form.get(\'review_text\', \'\').strip()\n\n    if restaurant_id == 0 or not customer_name or rating not in {\'1\',\'2\',\'3\',\'4\',\'5\'} or not review_text:\n        review_submission_status = \'Failed: Invalid input data\'\n        return render_template(\'write_review.html\', review_submission_status=review_submission_status, restaurant_options=[{\'restaurant_id\': r[\'restaurant_id\'], \'name\': r[\'name\']} for r in restaurants])\n\n    # Append new review\n    reviews = load_reviews()\n    max_review_id = max([r[\'review_id\'] for r in reviews], default=0)\n    new_review_id = max_review_id + 1\n    review_date = datetime.now().strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d\')\n\n    new_line = f"{new_review_id}|{restaurant_id}|{customer_name}|{rating}|{review_text}|{review_date}"\n    try:\n        with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, \'reviews.txt\'), \'a\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            f.write(new_line + \'\\n\')\n        review_submission_status = \'Review submitted successfully\'\n    except IOError:\n        review_submission_status = \'Failed to save review\'\n\n    return render_template(\'write_review.html\', review_submission_status=review_submission_status, restaurant_options=[{\'restaurant_id\': r[\'restaurant_id\'], \'name\': r[\'name\']} for r in restaurants])\n\n\nif __name__ == \'__main__\':\n    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)\n\n\n===           <button id="submit-review-button" type="submit">Submit Review</button>\n            </form>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n</body>\n</html>\n\n\n=== user_task_description ===\n\n# Requirements Document for \'FoodDelivery\' Web Application\n\n## 1. Objective\nDevelop a comprehensive web application named \'FoodDelivery\' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse restaurants, view menus, place food orders, track deliveries, and write reviews. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.\n\n## 2. Language\nThe required development language for the \'FoodDelivery\' application is Python.\n\n## 3. Page Design\n\nThe \'FoodDelivery\' web application will consist of the following nine pages:\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- **Page Title**: Food Delivery Dashboard\n- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured restaurants, popular cuisines, and quick navigation to all functionalities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.\n  - **ID: featured-restaurants** - Type: Div - Display of featured restaurant recommendations.\n  - **ID: browse-restaurants-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to restaurant listing page.\n  - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.\n  - **ID: active-orders-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to active orders page.\n\n### 2. Restaurant Listing Page\n- **Page Title**: Browse Restaurants\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all available restaurants with search and filter capabilities.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: restaurants-page** - Type: Div - Container for the restaurants page.\n  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search restaurants by name or cuisine type.\n  - **ID: cuisine-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by cuisine (Chinese, Italian, Indian, American, etc.).\n  - **ID: restaurants-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying restaurant cards with logo, name, rating, and delivery time.\n  - **ID: view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view restaurant menu (each restaurant card has this).\n\n### 3. Restaurant Menu Page\n- **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed menu items for a specific restaurant with descriptions and prices.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: menu-page** - Type: Div - Container for the menu page.\n  - **ID: restaurant-name** - Type: H1 - Display restaurant name.\n  - **ID: restaurant-info** - Type: Div - Display restaurant info (address, phone, rating).\n  - **ID: menu-items-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying menu items with photos, names, descriptions, and prices.\n  - **ID: add-to-cart-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add menu item to cart (each item has this).\n  - **ID: view-item-details-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view item details (each menu item has this).\n\n### 4. Item Details Page\n- **Page Title**: Item Details\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific menu item including ingredients and nutritional info.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: item-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the item details page.\n  - **ID: item-name** - Type: H1 - Display item name.\n  - **ID: item-description** - Type: Div - Display item description and ingredients.\n  - **ID: item-price** - Type: Div - Display item price.\n  - **ID: quantity-input** - Type: Input (number) - Field to select quantity before adding to cart.\n  - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add item with selected quantity to cart.\n\n### 5. Shopping Cart Page\n- **Page Title**: Shopping Cart\n- **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.\n  - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with name, quantity, price, and subtotal.\n  - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).\n  - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).\n  - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.\n  - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.\n\n### 6. Checkout Page\n- **Page Title**: Checkout\n- **Overview**: A page for users to enter delivery information and complete order placement.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.\n  - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.\n  - **ID: delivery-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input delivery address.\n  - **ID: phone-number** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.\n  - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, Cash, PayPal).\n  - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.\n\n### 7. Active Orders Page\n- **Page Title**: Active Orders\n- **Overview**: A page displaying current orders being prepared or delivered with tracking information.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: active-orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the active orders page.\n  - **ID: orders-list** - Type: Div - List displaying active orders with order ID, restaurant, status, and ETA.\n  - **ID: track-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view detailed tracking (each order has this).\n  - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Preparing, On the Way, Delivered).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n### 8. Order Tracking Page\n- **Page Title**: Track Order\n- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed order tracking information with delivery person details and real-time status updates.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.\n  - **ID: order-details** - Type: Div - Display complete order details and timeline.\n  - **ID: delivery-driver-info** - Type: Div - Display delivery driver name, phone, and vehicle info.\n  - **ID: estimated-time** - Type: Div - Display estimated delivery time.\n  - **ID: order-items-list** - Type: Div - List of items in the order.\n  - **ID: back-to-orders** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to active orders.\n\n### 9. Reviews Page\n- **Page Title**: Order Reviews\n- **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews for restaurants and allowing users to write new reviews.\n- **Elements**:\n  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.\n  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with restaurant name, rating, and review text.\n  - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.\n  - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).\n  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.\n\n## 4. Data Storage\n\nThe \'FoodDelivery\' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory \'data\'. The following data formats and examples are defined:\n\n### 1. Restaurants Data\n- **File Name**: `restaurants.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00\n  2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00\n  3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00\n  ```\n\n### 2. Menus Data\n- **File Name**: `menus.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1\n  2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1\n  3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1\n  ```\n\n### 3. Cart Data\n- **File Name**: `cart.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|2025-01-15\n  2|3|2|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n### 4. Orders Data\n- **File Name**: `orders.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234\n  2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678\n  ```\n\n### 5. Order Items Data\n- **File Name**: `order_items.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2|12.99\n  2|1|2|1|8.99\n  3|2|3|1|14.99\n  ```\n\n### 6. Deliveries Data\n- **File Name**: `deliveries.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45\n  2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30\n  ```\n\n### 7. Reviews Data\n- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`\n- **Data Format**:\n  ```\n  review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date\n  ```\n- **Example Data**:\n  ```\n  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12\n  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13\n  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n', request.form.get('customer_name', '').strip()     rating = request.form.get('rating', '').strip()     review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()      if restaurant_id == 0 or not customer_name or rating not in {'1','2','3','4','5'} or not review_text:         review_submission_status = 'Failed: Invalid input data'         return render_template('write_review.html', review_submission_status=review_submission_status, restaurant_options=[{'restaurant_id': r['restaurant_id'], 'name': r['name']} for r in restaurants])      # Append new review     reviews = load_reviews()     max_review_id = max([r['review_id'] for r in reviews], default=0)     new_review_id = max_review_id + 1     review_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')      new_line = f"{new_review_id}|{restaurant_id}|{customer_name}|{rating}|{review_text}|{review_date}"     try:         with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt'), 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:             f.write(new_line + '\n')         review_submission_status = 'Review submitted successfully'     except IOError:         review_submission_status = 'Failed to save review'      return render_template('write_review.html', review_submission_status=review_submission_status, restaurant_options=[{'restaurant_id': r['restaurant_id'], 'name': r['name']} for r in restaurants])   if   [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'FoodDelivery' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'FoodDelivery' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse restaurants, view menus, place food orders, track deliveries, and write reviews. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'FoodDelivery' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'FoodDelivery' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Food Delivery Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured restaurants, popular cuisines, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-restaurants** - Type: Div - Display of featured restaurant recommendations.   - **ID: browse-restaurants-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to restaurant listing page.   - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.   - **ID: active-orders-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to active orders page.  ### 2. Restaurant Listing Page - **Page Title**: Browse Restaurants - **Overview**: A page displaying all available restaurants with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: restaurants-page** - Type: Div - Container for the restaurants page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search restaurants by name or cuisine type.   - **ID: cuisine-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by cuisine (Chinese, Italian, Indian, American, etc.).   - **ID: restaurants-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying restaurant cards with logo, name, rating, and delivery time.   - **ID: view-restaurant-button-{restaurant_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view restaurant menu (each restaurant card has this).  ### 3. Restaurant Menu Page - **Page Title**: Restaurant Menu - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed menu items for a specific restaurant with descriptions and prices. - **Elements**:   - **ID: menu-page** - Type: Div - Container for the menu page.   - **ID: restaurant-name** - Type: H1 - Display restaurant name.   - **ID: restaurant-info** - Type: Div - Display restaurant info (address, phone, rating).   - **ID: menu-items-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying menu items with photos, names, descriptions, and prices.   - **ID: add-to-cart-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to add menu item to cart (each item has this).   - **ID: view-item-details-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view item details (each menu item has this).  ### 4. Item Details Page - **Page Title**: Item Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific menu item including ingredients and nutritional info. - **Elements**:   - **ID: item-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the item details page.   - **ID: item-name** - Type: H1 - Display item name.   - **ID: item-description** - Type: Div - Display item description and ingredients.   - **ID: item-price** - Type: Div - Display item price.   - **ID: quantity-input** - Type: Input (number) - Field to select quantity before adding to cart.   - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add item with selected quantity to cart.  ### 5. Shopping Cart Page - **Page Title**: Shopping Cart - **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option. - **Elements**:   - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.   - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with name, quantity, price, and subtotal.   - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).   - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).   - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.   - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.  ### 6. Checkout Page - **Page Title**: Checkout - **Overview**: A page for users to enter delivery information and complete order placement. - **Elements**:   - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.   - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.   - **ID: delivery-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input delivery address.   - **ID: phone-number** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.   - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, Cash, PayPal).   - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.  ### 7. Active Orders Page - **Page Title**: Active Orders - **Overview**: A page displaying current orders being prepared or delivered with tracking information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: active-orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the active orders page.   - **ID: orders-list** - Type: Div - List displaying active orders with order ID, restaurant, status, and ETA.   - **ID: track-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view detailed tracking (each order has this).   - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Preparing, On the Way, Delivered).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Order Tracking Page - **Page Title**: Track Order - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed order tracking information with delivery person details and real-time status updates. - **Elements**:   - **ID: tracking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the tracking page.   - **ID: order-details** - Type: Div - Display complete order details and timeline.   - **ID: delivery-driver-info** - Type: Div - Display delivery driver name, phone, and vehicle info.   - **ID: estimated-time** - Type: Div - Display estimated delivery time.   - **ID: order-items-list** - Type: Div - List of items in the order.   - **ID: back-to-orders** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to active orders.  ### 9. Reviews Page - **Page Title**: Order Reviews - **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews for restaurants and allowing users to write new reviews. - **Elements**:   - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.   - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with restaurant name, rating, and review text.   - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.   - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'FoodDelivery' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Restaurants Data - **File Name**: `restaurants.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   restaurant_id|name|cuisine|address|phone|rating|delivery_time|min_order   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Dragon House|Chinese|123 Main St|555-0001|4.5|30|15.00   2|La Bella Italia|Italian|456 Oak Ave|555-0002|4.8|25|20.00   3|Taj Mahal|Indian|789 Elm St|555-0003|4.6|35|18.00   ```  ### 2. Menus Data - **File Name**: `menus.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   item_id|restaurant_id|item_name|category|description|price|availability   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Fried Rice|Main Course|Steamed rice with vegetables and egg|12.99|1   2|1|Spring Rolls|Appetizer|Crispy rolls with pork filling|8.99|1   3|2|Spaghetti Carbonara|Pasta|Classic Italian pasta with cream sauce|14.99|1   ```  ### 3. Cart Data - **File Name**: `cart.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   cart_id|item_id|restaurant_id|quantity|added_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2|2025-01-15   2|3|2|1|2025-01-16   ```  ### 4. Orders Data - **File Name**: `orders.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   order_id|customer_name|restaurant_id|order_date|total_amount|status|delivery_address|phone_number   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|John Doe|1|2025-01-10|21.98|Delivered|123 Main St, NYC|555-1234   2|Jane Smith|2|2025-01-14|14.99|On the Way|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-5678   ```  ### 5. Order Items Data - **File Name**: `order_items.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   order_item_id|order_id|item_id|quantity|price   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2|12.99   2|1|2|1|8.99   3|2|3|1|14.99   ```  ### 6. Deliveries Data - **File Name**: `deliveries.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   delivery_id|order_id|driver_name|driver_phone|vehicle_info|status|estimated_time   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Mike Johnson|555-9001|Bike|Delivered|2025-01-10 18:45   2|2|Sarah Williams|555-9002|Car|On the Way|2025-01-14 19:30   ```  ### 7. Reviews Data - **File Name**: `reviews.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   review_id|restaurant_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Excellent food and fast delivery!|2025-01-12   2|2|Bob Williams|4|Great pasta, slightly delayed delivery.|2025-01-13   3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Best Indian food in town!|2025-01-15   ```

(POST)\n@app.route('/cart/update', methods=['POST'])\ndef update_cart():\n    # Expect fields of form: action, cart_id, quantity, item_id, restaurant_id\n    # Actions: 'update' (change quantity), 'remove' (remove item)\n\n    # This endpoint updated to handle update and remove by parsing form data accordingly\n    # The form uses names quantity-{item_id} for quantity inputs\n    # and remove-item=value for remove buttons\n\n    cart_items = load_cart()\n\n    # Process quantities update from all quantity-{item_id} input fields\n    quantities_update = {}\n    for key, value in request.form.items():\n        if key.startswith('quantity-'):\n            try:\n                item_id = int(key.split('-')[1])\n                qty = int(value)\n                if qty < 1:\n                    qty = 1\n                quantities_update[item_id] = qty\n            except (IndexError, ValueError):\n                continue\n\n    # Process remove item if any\n    remove_item_id = request.form.get('remove-item')\n\n    # Update cart.txt accordingly\n    new_lines = []\n    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'cart.txt')\n    try:\n        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in f:\n                parts = line.strip().split('|')\n                if len(parts) < 5:\n                    continue\n                try:\n                    cid = int(parts[0])\n                    item_id = int(parts[1])\n                except ValueError:\n                    continue\n\n                if remove_item_id and str(item_id) == remove_item_id:\n                    # Skip line to remove\n                    continue\n\n                # If item_id in quantities_update, update quantity\n                if item_id in quantities_update:\n                    parts[3] = str(quantities_update[item_id])\n\n                new_lines.append('|'.join(parts))\n    except IOError:\n        return redirect(url_for('shopping_cart_page'))\n\n    try:\n        with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in new_lines:\n                f.write(line + '\\n')\n    except IOError:\n        pass\n\n    return redirect(url_for('shopping_cart_page'))\n\n\n# 8. checkout_page (GET, POST)\n@app.route('/checkout', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef checkout_page():\n    if request.method == 'GET':\n        return
